function sensortag.CC2540 (peripheral)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540 = function (peripheral) {
  NobleDevice.call(this, peripheral);
  Common.call(this);

  this.type = 'cc2540';

  this.onAccelerometerChangeBinded      = this.onAccelerometerChange.bind(this);
  this.onMagnetometerChangeBinded       = this.onMagnetometerChange.bind(this);
  this.onGyroscopeChangeBinded          = this.onGyroscopeChange.bind(this);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.discover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.discover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = function(device) {
    constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);

    callback(device);
  };

  callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover = onDiscover;

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscover);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.discoverAll (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.discoverAll = function (callback) {
  constructor.emitter.addListener('discover', callback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 1) {
    noble.on('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.on('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    if (noble.state === 'poweredOn') {
      constructor.startScanning();
    }
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.discoverByAddress (address, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.discoverByAddress = function (address, callback) {
  constructor.discoverWithFilter(function(device) {
    return (device.address === address);
  }, callback);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.discoverWithFilter (filter, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.discoverWithFilter = function (filter, callback) {
  var onDiscoverWithFilter = function(device) {
    if (filter(device)) {
      constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);

      callback(device);
    }
  };

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.is (peripheral)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.is = function (peripheral) {
  var localName = peripheral.advertisement.localName;

  return (localName === 'SensorTag') ||
          (localName === 'TI BLE Sensor Tag');
}

function sensortag.CC2540.onDiscover (peripheral)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.onDiscover = function (peripheral) {
  if (constructor.is(peripheral)) {
    var device = new constructor(peripheral);

    constructor.emitter.emit('discover', device);
  }
}

    CC2540.onStateChange = function (state) {
  if (state === 'poweredOn' && constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length > 0) {
    constructor.startScanning();
  }

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertAccelerometerData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertAccelerometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt8(0) / 16.0;
  var y = data.readInt8(1) / 16.0;
  var z = data.readInt8(2) / 16.0;

  callback(x, y, z);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {

  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#Barometric_Pressure_Sensor_2
  var temp;     // Temperature raw value from sensor
  var pressure; // Pressure raw value from sensor
  var S;        // Interim value in calculation
  var O;        // Interim value in calculation
  var p_a;      // Pressure actual value in unit Pascal.
  var Pa;       // Computed value of the function

  var c0 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(0);
  var c1 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(2);
  var c2 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(4);
  var c3 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(6);

  var c4 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(8);
  var c5 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(10);
  var c6 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(12);
  var c7 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(14);

  temp = data.readInt16LE(0);
  pressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);

  S = c2 + ((c3 * temp)/ 131072.0) + ((c4 * (temp * temp)) / 17179869184.0);
  O = (c5 * 16384.0) + (((c6 * temp) / 8)) + ((c7 * (temp * temp)) / 524288.0);
  Pa = (((S * pressure) + O) / 16384.0);

  Pa /= 100.0;

  callback(Pa);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertGyroscopeData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertGyroscopeData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt16LE(0) * (500.0 / 65536.0) * -1;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(2) * (500.0 / 65536.0);
  var z = data.readInt16LE(4) * (500.0 / 65536.0);

  callback(x, y, z);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertHumidityData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -46.85 + 175.72 / 65536.0 * data.readUInt16LE(0);
  var humidity = -6.0 + 125.0 / 65536.0 * (data.readUInt16LE(2) & ~0x0003);

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData = function (data, callback) {
  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#IR_Temperature_Sensor

  var ambientTemperature = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;

  var Vobj2 = data.readInt16LE(0) * 0.00000015625;
  var Tdie2 = ambientTemperature + 273.15;
  var S0 = 5.593 * Math.pow(10, -14);
  var a1 = 1.75 * Math.pow(10 , -3);
  var a2 = -1.678 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b0 = -2.94 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b1 = -5.7 * Math.pow(10, -7);
  var b2 = 4.63 * Math.pow(10, -9);
  var c2 = 13.4;
  var Tref = 298.15;
  var S = S0 * (1 + a1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + a2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2));
  var Vos = b0 + b1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + b2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2);
  var fObj = (Vobj2 - Vos) + c2 * Math.pow((Vobj2 - Vos), 2);
  var objectTemperature = Math.pow(Math.pow(Tdie2, 4) + (fObj/S), 0.25);
  objectTemperature = (objectTemperature - 273.15);

  callback(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

  var y = data.readInt16LE(2) * 2000.0 / 65536.0;
  var z = data.readInt16LE(4) * 2000.0 / 65536.0;

  callback(x, y, z);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.enableBarometricPressure (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.enableBarometricPressure = function (callback) {
  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, 0x02, function(error) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CALIBRATION_UUID, function(error, data) {
      if (error) {
        return callback(error);
      }

      this._barometricPressureCalibrationData = data;

      this.enableConfigCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, callback);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.onGyroscopeChange (data)

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback) {
  period /= 10; // input is scaled by units of 10ms

  if (period < 1) {
    period = 1;
  } else if (period > 255) {
    period = 255;
  }

  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.stopDiscoverAll (discoverCallback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.stopDiscoverAll = function (discoverCallback) {
  constructor.emitter.removeListener('discover', discoverCallback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 0) {
    noble.removeListener('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.removeListener('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    constructor.stopScanning();
  }
}

function sensortag.CC2540.super_ (peripheral)

    function NobleDevice(peripheral) {
  this._peripheral = peripheral;
  this._services = {};
  this._characteristics = {};

  this.id = peripheral.id;
  this.uuid = peripheral.uuid; // for legacy
  this.address = peripheral.address;
  this.addressType = peripheral.addressType;
  this.connectedAndSetUp = false;
}

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.connect (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.connect = function (callback) {

  this._peripheral.connect(function(error) {
    if (!error) {
      this._peripheral.once('disconnect', this.onDisconnect.bind(this));
    }
    if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  }.bind(this));

}

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.connectAndSetup (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.connectAndSetup = function (callback) {
  this.connect(function(error) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics(function() {
      this.connectedAndSetUp = true;
      callback();
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}

  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics = function (callback) {
  this._peripheral.discoverAllServicesAndCharacteristics(function(error, services/*, characteristics*/) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    for (var i in services) {
      var service = services[i];
      var characteristics = service.characteristics;

      var serviceUuid = service.uuid;

      this._services[serviceUuid] = service;
      this._characteristics[serviceUuid] = {};

      for (var j in characteristics) {
        var characteristic = characteristics[j];

        this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristic.uuid] = characteristic;
      }
    }

    callback();
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.notifyCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.notifyCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  characteristic.notify(notify, function(error) {
    if (notify) {
      characteristic.addListener('data', listener);
    } else {
      characteristic.removeListener('data', listener);
    }

    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    n/a

  this.connectedAndSetUp = false;

}

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.readDataCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.readDataCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid].read(callback);
}
  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeDataCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.writeDataCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  var withoutResponse = (characteristic.properties.indexOf('writeWithoutResponse') !== -1) &&
                          (characteristic.properties.indexOf('write') === -1);

  characteristic.write(data, withoutResponse, function(error) {
    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeFloatLECharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.writeFloatLECharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback) {
  var buffer = new Buffer(4);
  buffer.writeFloatLE(value, 0);

  this.writeDataCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, buffer, callback);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeInt16LECharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2540.super_.prototype.writeInt16LECharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback) {
  var buffer = new Buffer(2);
  buffer.writeInt16LE(value, 0);

  this.writeDataCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, buffer, callback);

function sensortag.CC2650 (peripheral)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650 = function (peripheral) {
  NobleDevice.call(this, peripheral);
  Common.call(this);

  this.type = 'cc2650';
  this.mpu9250mask = 0;
  this.mpu9250notifyCount = 0;

  this.onMPU9250ChangeBinded     = this.onMPU9250Change.bind(this);
  this.onLuxometerChangeBinded   = this.onLuxometerChange.bind(this);
}

    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.discover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.discover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = function(device) {
    constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);

    callback(device);
  };

  callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover = onDiscover;

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscover);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.discoverAll (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.discoverAll = function (callback) {
  constructor.emitter.addListener('discover', callback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 1) {
    noble.on('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.on('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    if (noble.state === 'poweredOn') {
      constructor.startScanning();
    }
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.discoverWithFilter = function (filter, callback) {
  var onDiscoverWithFilter = function(device) {
    if (filter(device)) {
      constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);

      callback(device);
    }
  };

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {
  // data is returned as
  // Firmare 0.89 16 bit single precision float
  // Firmare 1.01 24 bit single precision float

  var flTempBMP;
  var flPressure;

  if (data.length > 4) {
    // Firmware 1.01

    flTempBMP = (data.readUInt32LE(0) & 0x00ffffff)/ 100.0;
    flPressure = ((data.readUInt32LE(2) >> 8) & 0x00ffffff) / 100.0;
  } else {
    // Firmware 0.89

    var tempBMP = data.readUInt16LE(0);
    var tempExponent = (tempBMP & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var tempMantissa = (tempBMP & 0x0FFF);
    flTempBMP = tempMantissa * Math.pow(2, tempExponent) / 100.0;

    var tempPressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);
    var pressureExponent = (tempPressure & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var pressureMantissa = (tempPressure & 0x0FFF);
    flPressure = pressureMantissa * Math.pow(2, pressureExponent) / 100.0;
  }

  callback(flPressure);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertHumidityData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -40 + ((165  * data.readUInt16LE(0)) / 65536.0);
  var humidity = data.readUInt16LE(2) * 100 / 65536.0;

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData = function (data, callback) {
  var ambientTemperature = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;
  var objectTemperature = data.readInt16LE(0) / 128.0;

  callback(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
}
  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertLuxometerData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertLuxometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var rawLux = data.readUInt16LE(0);

  var exponent = (rawLux & 0xF000) >> 12;
  var mantissa = (rawLux & 0x0FFF);

  var flLux = mantissa * Math.pow(2, exponent) / 100.0;

  callback(flLux);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertMPU9250Data (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertMPU9250Data = function (data, callback) {
  // 250 deg/s range
  var xG = data.readInt16LE(0) / 128.0;
  var yG = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;
  var zG = data.readInt16LE(4) / 128.0;

  // we specify 8G range in setup
  var x = data.readInt16LE(6) / 4096.0;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(8) / 4096.0;
  var z = data.readInt16LE(10) / 4096.0;

  // magnetometer (page 50 of http://www.invensense.com/mems/gyro/documents/RM-MPU-9250A-00.pdf)
  var xM = data.readInt16LE(12) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var yM = data.readInt16LE(14) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var zM = data.readInt16LE(16) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;

  callback(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;
  var reedRelay = (b & 0x4) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right, reedRelay);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.disableMPU9250 (mask, callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.disableMPU9250 = function (mask, callback) {
  this.mpu9250mask &= ~mask;

  if (this.mpu9250mask === 0) {
    this.writeUInt16LECharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_CONFIG_UUID, 0x0000, callback);
  } else if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
    callback();
  }
}

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.onMPU9250Change (data)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.onMPU9250Change = function (data) {
  this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM) {
    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_ACCELEROMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('accelerometerChange', x, y, z);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_GYROSCOPE_MASK) {
      this.emit('gyroscopeChange', xG, yG, zG);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_MAGNETOMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('magnetometerChange', xM, yM, zM);
    }
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.readAccelerometer (callback)

  • description and source-code
    CC2650.prototype.readAccelerometer = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z) {
      callback(null, x, y, z);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

    CC2650.stopDiscoverAll = function (discoverCallback) {
  constructor.emitter.removeListener('discover', discoverCallback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 0) {
    noble.removeListener('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.removeListener('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    constructor.stopScanning();
  }

function sensortag.discoverByAddress (address, callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverByAddress = function (address, callback) {
  address = address.toLowerCase();

  var onDiscoverByAddress = function(sensorTag) {
    if (sensorTag._peripheral.address === address) {
      SensorTag.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscoverByAddress);

      callback(sensorTag);
    }
  };

  SensorTag.discoverAll(onDiscoverByAddress);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.discoverAll (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverAll = function (callback) {
  constructor.emitter.addListener('discover', callback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 1) {
    noble.on('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.on('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    if (noble.state === 'poweredOn') {
      constructor.startScanning();
    }
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...

function sensortag.CC2540.stopDiscover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    stopDiscover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover;

  if (onDiscover) {
    constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.stopDiscoverAll (discoverCallback)

  • description and source-code
    stopDiscoverAll = function (discoverCallback) {
  constructor.emitter.removeListener('discover', discoverCallback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 0) {
    noble.removeListener('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.removeListener('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    constructor.stopScanning();
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...

    function NobleDevice(peripheral) {
  this._peripheral = peripheral;
  this._services = {};
  this._characteristics = {};

  this.id = peripheral.id;
  this.uuid = peripheral.uuid; // for legacy
  this.address = peripheral.address;
  this.addressType = peripheral.addressType;
  this.connectedAndSetUp = false;
}

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertAccelerometerData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertAccelerometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt8(0) / 16.0;
  var y = data.readInt8(1) / 16.0;
  var z = data.readInt8(2) / 16.0;

  callback(x, y, z);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {

  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#Barometric_Pressure_Sensor_2
  var temp;     // Temperature raw value from sensor
  var pressure; // Pressure raw value from sensor
  var S;        // Interim value in calculation
  var O;        // Interim value in calculation
  var p_a;      // Pressure actual value in unit Pascal.
  var Pa;       // Computed value of the function

  var c0 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(0);
  var c1 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(2);
  var c2 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(4);
  var c3 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(6);

  var c4 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(8);
  var c5 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(10);
  var c6 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(12);
  var c7 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(14);

  temp = data.readInt16LE(0);
  pressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);

  S = c2 + ((c3 * temp)/ 131072.0) + ((c4 * (temp * temp)) / 17179869184.0);
  O = (c5 * 16384.0) + (((c6 * temp) / 8)) + ((c7 * (temp * temp)) / 524288.0);
  Pa = (((S * pressure) + O) / 16384.0);

  Pa /= 100.0;

  callback(Pa);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
    callback(null, pressure);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onBarometricPressureChange = function(data) {
this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
...

    convertGyroscopeData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt16LE(0) * (500.0 / 65536.0) * -1;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(2) * (500.0 / 65536.0);
  var z = data.readInt16LE(4) * (500.0 / 65536.0);

  callback(x, y, z);
}

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertHumidityData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -46.85 + 175.72 / 65536.0 * data.readUInt16LE(0);
  var humidity = -6.0 + 125.0 / 65536.0 * (data.readUInt16LE(2) & ~0x0003);

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}
  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertIrTemperatureData = function (data, callback) {
  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#IR_Temperature_Sensor

  var ambientTemperature = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;

  var Vobj2 = data.readInt16LE(0) * 0.00000015625;
  var Tdie2 = ambientTemperature + 273.15;
  var S0 = 5.593 * Math.pow(10, -14);
  var a1 = 1.75 * Math.pow(10 , -3);
  var a2 = -1.678 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b0 = -2.94 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b1 = -5.7 * Math.pow(10, -7);
  var b2 = 4.63 * Math.pow(10, -9);
  var c2 = 13.4;
  var Tref = 298.15;
  var S = S0 * (1 + a1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + a2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2));
  var Vos = b0 + b1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + b2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2);
  var fObj = (Vobj2 - Vos) + c2 * Math.pow((Vobj2 - Vos), 2);
  var objectTemperature = Math.pow(Math.pow(Tdie2, 4) + (fObj/S), 0.25);
  objectTemperature = (objectTemperature - 273.15);

  callback(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readIrTemperature = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(IR_TEMPERATURE_UUID, IR_TEMPERATURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertIrTemperatureData(data, function(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature) {
    callback(null, objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

this.convertIrTemperatureData(data, function(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature) {
...

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right);
}

### Accelerometer

#### Enable/disable/configure

```javascript
sensorTag.enableAccelerometer(callback(error));

sensorTag.disableAccelerometer(callback(error));

// CC2540: period 1 - 2550 ms, default period is 2000 ms
// CC2650: period 100 - 2550 ms, default period is 1000 ms
sensorTag.setAccelerometerPeriod(period, callback(error));
```

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.enableBarometricPressure (callback)

  • description and source-code
    enableBarometricPressure = function (callback) {
  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, 0x02, function(error) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CALIBRATION_UUID, function(error, data) {
      if (error) {
        return callback(error);
      }

      this._barometricPressureCalibrationData = data;

      this.enableConfigCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, callback);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

### Barometric Pressure Sensor

#### Enable/disable

```javascript
sensorTag.enableBarometricPressure(callback(error));

sensorTag.disableBarometricPressure(callback(error));

sensorTag.setBarometricPressurePeriod(period, callback(error)); // period 100 - 2550 ms
```

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readAccelerometer (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readAccelerometer = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(ACCELEROMETER_UUID, ACCELEROMETER_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertAccelerometerData(data, function(x, y, z) {
      callback(null, x, y, z);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...
// CC2650: period 100 - 2550 ms, default period is 1000 ms
sensorTag.setAccelerometerPeriod(period, callback(error));

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readSystemId (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readSystemId = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(DEVICE_INFORMATION_UUID, SYSTEM_ID_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    var systemId = data.toString('hex').match(/.{1,2}/g).reverse().join(':');

    callback(null, systemId);
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

    setMagnetometerPeriod = function (period, callback) {
  this.writePeriodCharacteristic(MAGNETOMETER_UUID, MAGNETOMETER_PERIOD_UUID, period, callback);
}
  • example usage
    ...
```javascript
sensorTag.enableMagnetometer(callback(error));

sensorTag.disableMagnetometer(callback(error));

// CC2540: period 1 - 2550 ms, default period is 2000 ms
// CC2650: period 100 - 2550 ms, default period is 1000 ms
sensorTag.setMagnetometerPeriod(period, callback(error));
```

#### Read

```javascript
sensorTag.readMagnetometer(callback(error, x, y, z));
```

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writePeriodCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback) {
  period /= 10; // input is scaled by units of 10ms

  if (period < 1) {
    period = 1;
  } else if (period > 255) {
    period = 255;
  }

  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.disableConfigCharacteristic = function(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, callback) {
  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, 0x00, callback);
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.setIrTemperaturePeriod = function(period, callback) {

, callback);
};

};

  • description and source-code
    convertAccelerometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt8(0) / 16.0;
  var y = data.readInt8(1) / 16.0;
  var z = data.readInt8(2) / 16.0;

  callback(x, y, z);
}

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {

  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#Barometric_Pressure_Sensor_2
  var temp;     // Temperature raw value from sensor
  var pressure; // Pressure raw value from sensor
  var S;        // Interim value in calculation
  var O;        // Interim value in calculation
  var p_a;      // Pressure actual value in unit Pascal.
  var Pa;       // Computed value of the function

  var c0 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(0);
  var c1 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(2);
  var c2 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(4);
  var c3 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readUInt16LE(6);

  var c4 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(8);
  var c5 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(10);
  var c6 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(12);
  var c7 = this._barometricPressureCalibrationData.readInt16LE(14);

  temp = data.readInt16LE(0);
  pressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);

  S = c2 + ((c3 * temp)/ 131072.0) + ((c4 * (temp * temp)) / 17179869184.0);
  O = (c5 * 16384.0) + (((c6 * temp) / 8)) + ((c7 * (temp * temp)) / 524288.0);
  Pa = (((S * pressure) + O) / 16384.0);

  Pa /= 100.0;

  callback(Pa);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
    callback(null, pressure);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onBarometricPressureChange = function(data) {
this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
...

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertGyroscopeData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertGyroscopeData = function (data, callback) {
  var x = data.readInt16LE(0) * (500.0 / 65536.0) * -1;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(2) * (500.0 / 65536.0);
  var z = data.readInt16LE(4) * (500.0 / 65536.0);

  callback(x, y, z);
}

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertHumidityData

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertHumidityData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -46.85 + 175.72 / 65536.0 * data.readUInt16LE(0);
  var humidity = -6.0 + 125.0 / 65536.0 * (data.readUInt16LE(2) & ~0x0003);

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readHumidity = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(HUMIDITY_UUID, HUMIDITY_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertHumidityData(data, function(temperature, humidity) {
    callback(null, temperature, humidity);
  });
}.bind(this));
};

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertIrTemperatureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertIrTemperatureData = function (data, callback) {
  // For computation refer :  http://processors.wiki.ti.com/index.php/SensorTag_User_Guide#IR_Temperature_Sensor

  var ambientTemperature = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;

  var Vobj2 = data.readInt16LE(0) * 0.00000015625;
  var Tdie2 = ambientTemperature + 273.15;
  var S0 = 5.593 * Math.pow(10, -14);
  var a1 = 1.75 * Math.pow(10 , -3);
  var a2 = -1.678 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b0 = -2.94 * Math.pow(10, -5);
  var b1 = -5.7 * Math.pow(10, -7);
  var b2 = 4.63 * Math.pow(10, -9);
  var c2 = 13.4;
  var Tref = 298.15;
  var S = S0 * (1 + a1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + a2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2));
  var Vos = b0 + b1 * (Tdie2 - Tref) + b2 * Math.pow((Tdie2 - Tref), 2);
  var fObj = (Vobj2 - Vos) + c2 * Math.pow((Vobj2 - Vos), 2);
  var objectTemperature = Math.pow(Math.pow(Tdie2, 4) + (fObj/S), 0.25);
  objectTemperature = (objectTemperature - 273.15);

  callback(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readIrTemperature = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(IR_TEMPERATURE_UUID, IR_TEMPERATURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertIrTemperatureData(data, function(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature) {
    callback(null, objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onIrTemperatureChange = function(data) {
this.convertIrTemperatureData(data, function(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature) {
...

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.unnotifyBarometricPressure = function(callback) {

, callback);
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onSimpleKeyChange = function(data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));
};

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.enableBarometricPressure

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.enableBarometricPressure (callback)

  • description and source-code
    enableBarometricPressure = function (callback) {
  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, 0x02, function(error) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CALIBRATION_UUID, function(error, data) {
      if (error) {
        return callback(error);
      }

      this._barometricPressureCalibrationData = data;

      this.enableConfigCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_CONFIG_UUID, callback);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

    onSimpleKeyChange = function (data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readAccelerometer

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readAccelerometer (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readAccelerometer = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(ACCELEROMETER_UUID, ACCELEROMETER_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertAccelerometerData(data, function(x, y, z) {
      callback(null, x, y, z);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...
// CC2650: period 100 - 2550 ms, default period is 1000 ms
sensorTag.setAccelerometerPeriod(period, callback(error));
```

#### Read

```javascript
sensorTag.readAccelerometer(callback(error, x, y, z));
```

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readSystemId

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.readSystemId (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readSystemId = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(DEVICE_INFORMATION_UUID, SYSTEM_ID_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    var systemId = data.toString('hex').match(/.{1,2}/g).reverse().join(':');

    callback(null, systemId);
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

module sensortag.CC2540.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic

function sensortag.CC2540.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writePeriodCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback) {
  period /= 10; // input is scaled by units of 10ms

  if (period < 1) {
    period = 1;
  } else if (period > 255) {
    period = 255;
  }

module sensortag.CC2540.stopDiscoverAll

function sensortag.CC2540.stopDiscoverAll (discoverCallback)

  • description and source-code
    stopDiscoverAll = function (discoverCallback) {
  constructor.emitter.removeListener('discover', discoverCallback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 0) {
    noble.removeListener('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.removeListener('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    constructor.stopScanning();
  }
}

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.HeartRateMeasumentService.prototype.convertMeasument (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertMeasument = function (data, callback) {
  var flags = data.readUInt8(0);

  if (flags & 0x01) {
    // uint16
    callback(data.readUInt16LE(1));
  } else {
    // uint8
    callback(data.readUInt8(1));
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverServicesAndCharacteristics = function (callback) {
  this._peripheral.discoverAllServicesAndCharacteristics(function(error, services/*, characteristics*/) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    for (var i in services) {
      var service = services[i];
      var characteristics = service.characteristics;

      var serviceUuid = service.uuid;

      this._services[serviceUuid] = service;
      this._characteristics[serviceUuid] = {};

      for (var j in characteristics) {
        var characteristic = characteristics[j];

        this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristic.uuid] = characteristic;
      }
    }

    callback();
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.hasCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)

  • description and source-code
    hasCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid) {
  return this.hasService(serviceUuid) && (!!this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid]);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.notifyCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback)

  • description and source-code
    notifyCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  characteristic.notify(notify, function(error) {
    if (notify) {
      characteristic.addListener('data', listener);
    } else {
      characteristic.removeListener('data', listener);
    }

    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...
SensorTagCommon.prototype.onIrTemperatureChange = function(data) {
  this.convertIrTemperatureData(data, function(objectTemperature, ambientTemperature) {
    this.emit('irTemperatureChange', objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
  }.bind(this));
};

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeDataCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writeDataCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  var withoutResponse = (characteristic.properties.indexOf('writeWithoutResponse') !== -1) &&
                          (characteristic.properties.indexOf('write') === -1);

  characteristic.write(data, withoutResponse, function(error) {
    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeFloatLECharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writeFloatLECharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, value, callback) {
  var buffer = new Buffer(4);
  buffer.writeFloatLE(value, 0);

  this.writeDataCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, buffer, callback);
}

module sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.discoverServicesAndCharacteristics (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverServicesAndCharacteristics = function (callback) {
  this._peripheral.discoverAllServicesAndCharacteristics(function(error, services/*, characteristics*/) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    for (var i in services) {
      var service = services[i];
      var characteristics = service.characteristics;

      var serviceUuid = service.uuid;

      this._services[serviceUuid] = service;
      this._characteristics[serviceUuid] = {};

      for (var j in characteristics) {
        var characteristic = characteristics[j];

        this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristic.uuid] = characteristic;
      }
    }

    callback();
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

module sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.notifyCharacteristic

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.notifyCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback)

  • description and source-code
    notifyCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, notify, listener, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  characteristic.notify(notify, function(error) {
    if (notify) {
      characteristic.addListener('data', listener);
    } else {
      characteristic.removeListener('data', listener);
    }

    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...

    this.emit('irTemperatureChange', objectTemperature, ambientTemperature);
  }.bind(this));
};

module sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeDataCharacteristic

function sensortag.CC2540.super_.prototype.writeDataCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writeDataCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, data, callback) {
  if (!this.hasService(serviceUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('service uuid ' + serviceUuid + ' not found!'));
  } else if (!this.hasCharacteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid)) {
    return callback(new Error('characteristic uuid ' + characteristicUuid + ' not found in service uuid ' + serviceUuid + '!'));
  }

  var characteristic = this._characteristics[serviceUuid][characteristicUuid];

  var withoutResponse = (characteristic.properties.indexOf('writeWithoutResponse') !== -1) &&
                          (characteristic.properties.indexOf('write') === -1);

  characteristic.write(data, withoutResponse, function(error) {
    if (typeof callback === 'function') {
      callback(error);
    }
  });
}
  • example usage
    n/a

  • description and source-code
    discover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = function(device) {
    constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);

    callback(device);

  callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover = onDiscover;

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscover);
}

function sensortag.CC2650.discoverAll (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverAll = function (callback) {
  constructor.emitter.addListener('discover', callback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 1) {
    noble.on('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.on('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    if (noble.state === 'poweredOn') {
      constructor.startScanning();
    }
  }
}
  • example usage

    function NobleDevice(peripheral) {
  this._peripheral = peripheral;
  this._services = {};
  this._characteristics = {};

  this.id = peripheral.id;
  this.uuid = peripheral.uuid; // for legacy
  this.address = peripheral.address;
  this.addressType = peripheral.addressType;

module sensortag.CC2650.discover

function sensortag.CC2650.discover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discover = function (callback) {

  };

  callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover = onDiscover;

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscover);
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

### Discover

module sensortag.CC2650.discoverAll

function sensortag.CC2650.discoverAll (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverAll = function (callback) {
  constructor.emitter.addListener('discover', callback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 1) {
    noble.on('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.on('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    if (noble.state === 'poweredOn') {
      constructor.startScanning();
    }
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...
#### All

function onDiscover(sensorTag) {
  // ...
}

SensorTag.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);
```

    return (device.address === address);

module sensortag.CC2650.discoverWithFilter

function sensortag.CC2650.discoverWithFilter (filter, callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverWithFilter = function (filter, callback) {
  var onDiscoverWithFilter = function(device) {
    if (filter(device)) {
      constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);

      callback(device);
    }
  };

  constructor.discoverAll(onDiscoverWithFilter);
}

module sensortag.CC2650.is

function sensortag.CC2650.is (peripheral)

  • description and source-code
    is = function (peripheral) {
  var localName = peripheral.advertisement.localName;
  var serviceUuids = peripheral.advertisement.serviceUuids;

  return (localName === 'CC2650 SensorTag') || (localName === 'SensorTag 2.0') || (serviceUuids.indexOf('aa80') > -1 );
}

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {
  // data is returned as
  // Firmare 0.89 16 bit single precision float
  // Firmare 1.01 24 bit single precision float

  var flTempBMP;
  var flPressure;

  if (data.length > 4) {
    // Firmware 1.01

    flTempBMP = (data.readUInt32LE(0) & 0x00ffffff)/ 100.0;
    flPressure = ((data.readUInt32LE(2) >> 8) & 0x00ffffff) / 100.0;
  } else {
    // Firmware 0.89

    var tempBMP = data.readUInt16LE(0);
    var tempExponent = (tempBMP & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var tempMantissa = (tempBMP & 0x0FFF);
    flTempBMP = tempMantissa * Math.pow(2, tempExponent) / 100.0;

    var tempPressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);
    var pressureExponent = (tempPressure & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var pressureMantissa = (tempPressure & 0x0FFF);
    flPressure = pressureMantissa * Math.pow(2, pressureExponent) / 100.0;
  }

  callback(flPressure);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
    callback(null, pressure);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onBarometricPressureChange = function(data) {
this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
...

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertHumidityData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -40 + ((165  * data.readUInt16LE(0)) / 65536.0);
  var humidity = data.readUInt16LE(2) * 100 / 65536.0;

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertLuxometerData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertLuxometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var rawLux = data.readUInt16LE(0);

  var exponent = (rawLux & 0xF000) >> 12;
  var mantissa = (rawLux & 0x0FFF);

  var flLux = mantissa * Math.pow(2, exponent) / 100.0;

  callback(flLux);
}
  • example usage

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertMPU9250Data (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertMPU9250Data = function (data, callback) {
  // 250 deg/s range
  var xG = data.readInt16LE(0) / 128.0;
  var yG = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;
  var zG = data.readInt16LE(4) / 128.0;

  // we specify 8G range in setup
  var x = data.readInt16LE(6) / 4096.0;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(8) / 4096.0;
  var z = data.readInt16LE(10) / 4096.0;

  // magnetometer (page 50 of http://www.invensense.com/mems/gyro/documents/RM-MPU-9250A-00.pdf)
  var xM = data.readInt16LE(12) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var yM = data.readInt16LE(14) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var zM = data.readInt16LE(16) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;

  callback(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;
  var reedRelay = (b & 0x4) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right, reedRelay);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.unnotifyBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
  this.notifyCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, false, this.onBarometricPressureChangeBinded
, callback);
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onSimpleKeyChange = function(data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));
};

    disableMPU9250 = function (mask, callback) {
  this.mpu9250mask &= ~mask;

  if (this.mpu9250mask === 0) {
    this.writeUInt16LECharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_CONFIG_UUID, 0x0000, callback);
  } else if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
    callback();
  }

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.onMPU9250Change (data)

  • description and source-code
    onMPU9250Change = function (data) {
  this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM) {
    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_ACCELEROMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('accelerometerChange', x, y, z);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_GYROSCOPE_MASK) {
      this.emit('gyroscopeChange', xG, yG, zG);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_MAGNETOMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('magnetometerChange', xM, yM, zM);
    }
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.onSimpleKeyChange (data)

  • description and source-code
    onSimpleKeyChange = function (data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.readAccelerometer (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readAccelerometer = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z) {
      callback(null, x, y, z);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...
// CC2650: period 100 - 2550 ms, default period is 1000 ms
sensorTag.setAccelerometerPeriod(period, callback(error));
```

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.readSystemId (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readSystemId = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(DEVICE_INFORMATION_UUID, SYSTEM_ID_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    var systemId = data.toString('hex').match(/.{1,2}/g).reverse().join(':');

    callback(null, systemId);
  });
}
  • example usage
    ...
```

sensorTag.readSystemId(callback(error, systemId));

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.unnotifyMPU9250 (callback)

  • description and source-code
    unnotifyMPU9250 = function (callback) {
  this.mpu9250notifyCount--;

  if (this.mpu9250notifyCount === 0) {
    this.notifyCharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_DATA_UUID, false, this.onMPU9250ChangeBinded, callback);
  } else if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
    callback();
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writePeriodCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback) {
  period /= 10; // input is scaled by units of 10ms

  if (period < 1) {
    period = 1;
  } else if (period > 255) {
    period = 255;
  }

  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, 0x00, callback);
};

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertBarometricPressureData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertBarometricPressureData = function (data, callback) {
  // data is returned as
  // Firmare 0.89 16 bit single precision float
  // Firmare 1.01 24 bit single precision float

  var flTempBMP;
  var flPressure;

  if (data.length > 4) {
    // Firmware 1.01

    flTempBMP = (data.readUInt32LE(0) & 0x00ffffff)/ 100.0;
    flPressure = ((data.readUInt32LE(2) >> 8) & 0x00ffffff) / 100.0;
  } else {
    // Firmware 0.89

    var tempBMP = data.readUInt16LE(0);
    var tempExponent = (tempBMP & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var tempMantissa = (tempBMP & 0x0FFF);
    flTempBMP = tempMantissa * Math.pow(2, tempExponent) / 100.0;

    var tempPressure = data.readUInt16LE(2);
    var pressureExponent = (tempPressure & 0xF000) >> 12;
    var pressureMantissa = (tempPressure & 0x0FFF);
    flPressure = pressureMantissa * Math.pow(2, pressureExponent) / 100.0;
  }

  callback(flPressure);
}
  • example usage
    ...

SensorTagCommon.prototype.readBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
  if (error) {
    return callback(error);
  }

  this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
    callback(null, pressure);
  }.bind(this));
}.bind(this));
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onBarometricPressureChange = function(data) {
this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
...

    convertHumidityData = function (data, callback) {
  var temperature = -40 + ((165  * data.readUInt16LE(0)) / 65536.0);
  var humidity = data.readUInt16LE(2) * 100 / 65536.0;

  callback(temperature, humidity);
}

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertLuxometerData

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertLuxometerData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertLuxometerData = function (data, callback) {
  var rawLux = data.readUInt16LE(0);

  var exponent = (rawLux & 0xF000) >> 12;
  var mantissa = (rawLux & 0x0FFF);

  var flLux = mantissa * Math.pow(2, exponent) / 100.0;

  callback(flLux);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertMPU9250Data

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertMPU9250Data (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertMPU9250Data = function (data, callback) {
  // 250 deg/s range
  var xG = data.readInt16LE(0) / 128.0;
  var yG = data.readInt16LE(2) / 128.0;
  var zG = data.readInt16LE(4) / 128.0;

  // we specify 8G range in setup
  var x = data.readInt16LE(6) / 4096.0;
  var y = data.readInt16LE(8) / 4096.0;
  var z = data.readInt16LE(10) / 4096.0;

  // magnetometer (page 50 of http://www.invensense.com/mems/gyro/documents/RM-MPU-9250A-00.pdf)
  var xM = data.readInt16LE(12) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var yM = data.readInt16LE(14) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;
  var zM = data.readInt16LE(16) * 4912.0 / 32768.0;

  callback(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM);
}
  • example usage
    n/a

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;
  var reedRelay = (b & 0x4) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right, reedRelay);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.unnotifyBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
  this.notifyCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, false, this.onBarometricPressureChangeBinded
, callback);
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onSimpleKeyChange = function(data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));
};

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.disableMPU9250

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.disableMPU9250 (mask, callback)

  • description and source-code
    disableMPU9250 = function (mask, callback) {
  this.mpu9250mask &= ~mask;

  if (this.mpu9250mask === 0) {
    this.writeUInt16LECharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_CONFIG_UUID, 0x0000, callback);
  } else if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
    callback();
  }
}

module sensortag.CC2650.prototype.onMPU9250Change

function sensortag.CC2650.prototype.onMPU9250Change (data)

  • description and source-code
    onMPU9250Change = function (data) {
  this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z, xG, yG, zG, xM, yM, zM) {
    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_ACCELEROMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('accelerometerChange', x, y, z);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_GYROSCOPE_MASK) {
      this.emit('gyroscopeChange', xG, yG, zG);
    }

    if (this.mpu9250mask & MPU9250_MAGNETOMETER_MASK) {
      this.emit('magnetometerChange', xM, yM, zM);
    }
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    n/a

    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertMPU9250Data(data, function(x, y, z) {
      callback(null, x, y, z);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}

  • description and source-code
    unnotifyMPU9250 = function (callback) {
  this.mpu9250notifyCount--;

  if (this.mpu9250notifyCount === 0) {
    this.notifyCharacteristic(MPU9250_UUID, MPU9250_DATA_UUID, false, this.onMPU9250ChangeBinded, callback);
  } else if (typeof(callback) === 'function') {
    callback();
  }
}

module sensortag.CC2650.stopDiscover

function sensortag.CC2650.stopDiscover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    stopDiscover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = callback._nobleDeviceOnDiscover;

  if (onDiscover) {
    constructor.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);
  }
}
  • example usage
    n/a

module sensortag.CC2650.stopDiscoverAll

function sensortag.CC2650.stopDiscoverAll (discoverCallback)

  • description and source-code
    stopDiscoverAll = function (discoverCallback) {
  constructor.emitter.removeListener('discover', discoverCallback);

  if (constructor.emitter.listeners('discover').length === 0) {
    noble.removeListener('discover', constructor.onDiscover);
    noble.removeListener('stateChange', constructor.onStateChange);

    constructor.stopScanning();
  }
}
  • example usage
    ...
```javascript
function onDiscover(sensorTag) {
  // ...
}

SensorTag.discoverAll(onDiscover);

SensorTag.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);
```

module sensortag.common.prototype

function sensortag.common.prototype.convertSimpleKeyData (data, callback)

  • description and source-code
    convertSimpleKeyData = function (data, callback) {
  var b = data.readUInt8(0);

  var left = (b & 0x2) ? true : false;
  var right = (b & 0x1) ? true : false;

  callback(left, right);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.unnotifyBarometricPressure = function(callback) {
  this.notifyCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, false, this.onBarometricPressureChangeBinded
, callback);
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.onSimpleKeyChange = function(data) {
  this.convertSimpleKeyData(data, function(/*left, right, ...*/) {
    var emitArguments = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments);
    emitArguments.unshift('simpleKeyChange');

    this.emit.apply(this, emitArguments);
  }.bind(this));
};

function sensortag.common.prototype.readBarometricPressure (callback)

  • description and source-code
    readBarometricPressure = function (callback) {
  this.readDataCharacteristic(BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_UUID, BAROMETRIC_PRESSURE_DATA_UUID, function(error, data) {
    if (error) {
      return callback(error);
    }

    this.convertBarometricPressureData(data, function(pressure) {
      callback(null, pressure);
    }.bind(this));
  }.bind(this));
}
  • example usage
    ...

sensorTag.setBarometricPressurePeriod(period, callback(error)); // period 100 - 2550 ms

function sensortag.common.prototype.writePeriodCharacteristic (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback)

  • description and source-code
    writePeriodCharacteristic = function (serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback) {
  period /= 10; // input is scaled by units of 10ms

  if (period < 1) {
    period = 1;
  } else if (period > 255) {
    period = 255;
  }

  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, period, callback);
}
  • example usage
    ...
};

SensorTagCommon.prototype.disableConfigCharacteristic = function(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, callback) {
  this.writeUInt8Characteristic(serviceUuid, characteristicUuid, 0x00, callback);
};

  this.writePeriodCharacteristic(IR_TEMPERATURE_UUID, IR_TEMPERATURE_PERIOD_UUID, period
, callback);
};

  this.enableConfigCharacteristic(IR_TEMPERATURE_UUID, IR_TEMPERATURE_CONFIG_UUID, callback);
};

function sensortag.discover (callback)

  • description and source-code
    discover = function (callback) {
  var onDiscover = function(sensorTag) {
    SensorTag.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscover);

    callback(sensorTag);
  };

  SensorTag.discoverAll(onDiscover);
}

module sensortag.discoverAll

function sensortag.discoverAll (onDiscover)

module sensortag.discoverByAddress

function sensortag.discoverByAddress (address, callback)

  • description and source-code
    discoverByAddress = function (address, callback) {
  address = address.toLowerCase();

  var onDiscoverByAddress = function(sensorTag) {
    if (sensorTag._peripheral.address === address) {
      SensorTag.stopDiscoverAll(onDiscoverByAddress);

      callback(sensorTag);
    }
  };

  SensorTag.discoverAll(onDiscoverByAddress);
}
  • example usage
    ...
